if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: ajax.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): ajax.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('ajax.php') != '6e2045f3fd200b422ef6852a8556631a811d6d65') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('ajax.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of ajax.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '6e2045f3fd200b422ef6852a8556631a811d6d65') {
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '4a485a4cd542cf054db42fe5dc28921ba1a45d95') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: ajax.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('ajax.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '6e2045f3fd200b422ef6852a8556631a811d6d65') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/database/odbc/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionODBC.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/database/odbc/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionODBC.class.php') !== '4b25be55c92f81d12976d7cbf8dfbd220016999d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/database/odbc/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionODBC.class.php');
		}
	}
}

	}

	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'a7e09960a98416dd7a8178192c1ec99b39c9877a') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '5fba0127a10aa6e2c4c859b5687a8f31ecfdac87') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'a7e09960a98416dd7a8178192c1ec99b39c9877a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}
